  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_41cd92a9-38a0-489d-b022-830c37065823'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();

  <span id="freeText15756451687864186189" style="display:none">This was a lot shorter than I imagined, but it definitely gives you the Divergent feels even though plotwise everything has been covered in the previous books. <br><br><i> "You’re the one who has to live with your choice." <br>"Everyone else will get over it, move on, no matter what you decide. But you never will." </i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1508147180i/24185207._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The transfer follows Tobias from the day of his aptitude test and though his Choosing day until the moment he´s given his infamous nickname- Four. It gives you a better understanding of the choice he made, and why he chose dauntless as apposed to any of the other factions. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1508147180ra/24185208.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>It´s not the same Tobias you meet in Divergent, nor the same voice you follow in Allegiant, this is Tobias before he became Four.<br><br><i> "Trust me when I tell you, Eaton boy, that resisting is worth doing." </i> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1508147180ra/24185206.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_718189834" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/718189834" />
    <a title="karen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/45618-karen"><img alt="karen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1596291582p2/45618.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/718189834?book_show_action=true">Sep 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="karen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="karen" href="/user/show/45618-karen">karen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/45618-karen?shelf=continuations-n-retellings">continuations-n-retellings</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/45618-karen?shelf=why-yes-i-ya">why-yes-i-ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/45618-karen?shelf=hey-shorty">hey-shorty</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer718189834" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14501813631824076160">veronica roth is so smart. <br/><br/>not only is she releasing, in measured intervals, four novellas (four about FOUR!! get it??) that lead <i>right</i> up to the release date for the <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13335037.Divergent__Divergent___1_' title='Divergent (Divergent, #1) by Veronica Roth' rel='nofollow noopener'>Divergent</a> movie in march, but she is being smart about <i>how</i> she writes them. <br/><br/>i wasn't crazy about <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13615258.Free_Four_Tobias_Tells_the_Divergent_Knife_Throwing_Scene__Divergent___1_5_' title='Free Four Tobias Tells the Divergent Knife-Throwing Scene (Divergent, #1.5) by Veronica Roth' rel='nofollow noopener'>Free Four: Tobias Tells the Story</a>, but this one is fantastic. with <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13615258.Free_Four_Tobias_Tells_the_Divergent_Knife_Throwing_Scene__Divergent___1_5_' title='Free Four Tobias Tells the Divergent Knife-Throwing Scene (Divergent, #1.5) by Veronica Roth' rel='nofollow noopener'>Free Four: Tobias Tells the Story</a>, she just retold a scene from <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13335037.Divergent__Divergent___1_' title='Divergent (Divergent, #1) by Veronica Roth' rel='nofollow noopener'>Divergent</a> from tobias' perspective. which is nice, but since i am too old to be crushing on a (teenage) c</span>
  <span id="freeText14501813631824076160" style="display:none">veronica roth is so smart. <br><br>not only is she releasing, in measured intervals, four novellas (four about FOUR!! get it??) that lead <i>right</i> up to the release date for the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13335037.Divergent__Divergent___1_" title="Divergent (Divergent, #1) by Veronica Roth" rel="nofollow noopener">Divergent</a> movie in march, but she is being smart about <i>how</i> she writes them. <br><br>i wasn't crazy about <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13615258.Free_Four_Tobias_Tells_the_Divergent_Knife_Throwing_Scene__Divergent___1_5_" title="Free Four Tobias Tells the Divergent Knife-Throwing Scene (Divergent, #1.5) by Veronica Roth" rel="nofollow noopener">Free Four: Tobias Tells the Story</a>, but this one is fantastic. with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13615258.Free_Four_Tobias_Tells_the_Divergent_Knife_Throwing_Scene__Divergent___1_5_" title="Free Four Tobias Tells the Divergent Knife-Throwing Scene (Divergent, #1.5) by Veronica Roth" rel="nofollow noopener">Free Four: Tobias Tells the Story</a>, she just retold a scene from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13335037.Divergent__Divergent___1_" title="Divergent (Divergent, #1) by Veronica Roth" rel="nofollow noopener">Divergent</a> from tobias' perspective. which is nice, but since i am too old to be crushing on a (teenage) character from a book, i didn't get all whoopty-blah about it. it was fine, and i love that it exists for the more age-appropriate fans to swoon over, but it didn't really work for me as a reader. <br><br>but this one did. and going by my two-years-ago memory of reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13335037.Divergent__Divergent___1_" title="Divergent (Divergent, #1) by Veronica Roth" rel="nofollow noopener">Divergent</a> (and reading other people's reviews of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18080920.The_Transfer__Divergent___0_1_" title="The Transfer (Divergent, #0.1) by Veronica Roth" rel="nofollow noopener">The Transfer: A Divergent Story</a>, thank you all) there isn't any new, revelatory material here. everything here, plotwise, has been covered in the previous books. but roth fleshed out the bones of known backstory with that meat of fiction: character. and it reminded me why i liked <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13335037.Divergent__Divergent___1_" title="Divergent (Divergent, #1) by Veronica Roth" rel="nofollow noopener">Divergent</a> so much. so it works as a refresher: "this is why you liked this character, remember?? this is where he is coming from and what he has experienced. and this is how i write, which is not the most poetic or original style in the world, but it is with a powerful sense of sympathy and immediacy. and you like that."<br><br>so it's great to have this memory-blast, and i assume the three forthcoming ones will be the same kind of thing - where we aren't being given new material, just enhanced, already-known plot, which doesn't come across as redundant because of all the added surrounding detail, but which also means that a fan without access to e-books isn't going to be deprived of actual content if they aren't able to read them. <br><br>smart, smart, smart.<br><br>what is not smart is this casting. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380436441i/882118._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>now, according to my imdb-and-math skills, this guy is only 24, and tobias is supposed to be 18, but this actor looks so much older than 24, right? this isn't a kid, this is a full-on grown-up <i>dude</i>.<br><br>"i do not care for it" i sniff petulantly.<br><br>but i did care for this story. and i will gladly be snatching up the other three. <br><br>WOOT!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1528725630i/25720315.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><a href="http://bloggycomelately.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">come to my blog!</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="14501813631824076160" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <span id="freeText10737149240882217491" style="display:none"><b>Sep 03, 2013 (before reading)</b><br />A fat cow never goes unmilked… and so here it comes the army of overpriced short stories.<br /><br />Kindle Price: $2.06<br />Print Length: 30 pages<br /><br />Seriously.<br /><br /><br /><b>Oct 26, 2013 (after reading)</b><br />Just for clarity's sake: on my ADE reader, the ebook was exactly 34 pages long, and the story began on page 4 (Four! Hey, you did a job, you have to get paid.<br />But this story is more like a marketing aid for the actual books of the series (and the upcoming movie!), and for this price it should be doubly as long as it is.<br /><br />That being said… yes, I liked it.</span>

How did I not know these novellas existed? I know, I'm really late to the party but I'm here now, that's what matters right? Anywho, I really enjoyed reading this and I absolutely love having his POV it was great being inside his head. It was nice getting more back story on Tobias's relationship with his father Marcus too, who may I remind you is a complete POS!!! It was really kinda strange to see such a vulnerable side to him and to see the fear and the struggles he had. I liked seeing this thought process on the whole Choosing Ceremony and how he came to the decision to join Dauntless. Though I do think this was a lot like Tris's story once Tobias joined Dauntless. Wish it would have played out a bit different but nonetheless, it was still interesting. Most of all I loved the bit at the end, finding out how he got his nickname FOUR.❤<br><br>Moving on to #0.2 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18668485.The_Initiate__Divergent___0_2_" title="The Initiate (Divergent, #0.2) by Veronica Roth" rel="nofollow noopener">The Initiate</a>, CAN'T WAIT!!!!</span>

  <span id="freeText6402193222039061921" style="display:none">Q: “This train stops for no one.” (c)<br />Q: A new knife for each person, and a new choice. (c)<br /><br />Freedom. Choice. Inertia. Aptitudes. Strenghth.<br /><br />Q:<br />“Trust me when I tell you, Eaton boy, that resisting is worth doing.” (c)<br />Q:<br />Sometimes I know people are lying just because of the way the words feel when they press into me, uncomfortable and wrong, the way an Erudite feels when she reads a grammatically incorrect sentence. (c)<br />Q:<br />I sit with my hands clenching my knees, watching the other tables, while the other students finish their aptitude tests. The Erudite table is covered in reading material, but they aren’t all studying—they’re just making a show of it, trading conversation instead of ideas, their eyes snapping back to the words every time they think someone’s watching them. The Candor are talking loudly, as always. The Amity are laughing, smiling, pulling food from their pockets and passing it around. The Dauntless are raucous and loud, slung over the tables and chairs, leaning on one another and poking one another and teasing.<br />I wanted any other faction. Any other faction but mine, where everyone has already decided that I am not worth their attention. (c)<br />Q:<br />But there is something appealing about it here too, a freedom, a refusal to belong to these arbitrary categories we’ve made for ourselves. (c)<br />Q:<br />“I’m not supposed to tell anyone,” I say automatically.<br />“I’m not anyone,” he says. “I’m nobody. That’s what being factionless is.” (c)<br />Q:<br />My mother was the one who taught me to steal moments like those, moments of freedom, though she didn’t know it. (c)<br />Q:<br />... I have filled the trunk with objects that others would call useless: old spectacles without glass in them, fragments of discarded motherboards, spark plugs, stripped wires, the broken neck of a green bottle, a rusted knife blade. I don’t know if my mother would have called them beautiful, or even if I would, but each of them struck me the same way that sculpture did, as secret things, and valuable ones, if only because they were so overlooked. (c)<br />Q:<br />In Amity I would find the kind of acceptance I’ve craved my entire life, and maybe, over time, it would teach me to feel steady in myself, comfortable with who I am. <br />But as I look at the people sitting in that section, in their reds and yellows, I see only whole, healed people, capable of cheering one another, capable of supporting one another. They are too perfect, too kind, for someone like me to be driven into their arms by rage and fear. (c)<br />Q:<br />It never occurred to me before that I could refuse to give my name, or that I could give a false one, construct a new identity for myself. I’m free here, free to snap at people and free to refuse them and free even to lie. (c)<br />Q:<br />If I strike at their memories now, as hard as I can, become as memorable as my Dauntless self as possible, I can maybe save myself. (c)</span>

  <span id="freeText14239546755046659592" style="display:none"><b>2.5 stars - Spoilers</b><br /><br />Meh, it was mostly boring. The storyline was decent enough with Tobias wanting to escape his abusive dad, thus transferring to Dauntless, and then jumping off trains and buildings to prove himself, and finally facing his fears in a scientifically nonsensical simulation. <br />I really wasn't impressed with Four's narration — his voice was too dull and predictable, and it ruined the story.<br />I predict that he'll probably fall for a fellow Dauntless initiate in one of his future novellas, and then she'll die or some rubbish. I hope that doesn't happen though, it's way too cliched.<br /></span>

Yeah, go for it!</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15271339250257020412"><br/><b> <i> "My name is Four." I say. "Call me 'Stiff' again and you and I will have a problem." </i></b> <br/><br/>My Reaction before reading this novella:<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380428336ra/857032.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>My reaction while reading:<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393061ra/756703.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380382664ra/740605.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Can you freaking believe it??!! Veronica granted Four fans greatest wish EVERYWHERE. It's like Christmas came so EARLY this year! Tobias Eaton is probably one of the most coveted, crushed-on, daydreamed-on male YA character today. His mysterious badass vibe made its first steamy appearance way back 2011 on <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13335037.Divergent__Divergent___1_' title='Divergent (Divergent, #1) by Veronica Roth' rel='nofollow noopener'>Divergent</a>. The first novella written i</span>
  <span id="freeText15271339250257020412" style="display:none"><br><b> <i> "My name is Four." I say. "Call me 'Stiff' again and you and I will have a problem." </i></b> <br><br>My Reaction before reading this novella:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380428336ra/857032.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>My reaction while reading:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393061ra/756703.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380382664ra/740605.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Can you freaking believe it??!! Veronica granted Four fans greatest wish EVERYWHERE. It's like Christmas came so EARLY this year! Tobias Eaton is probably one of the most coveted, crushed-on, daydreamed-on male YA character today. His mysterious badass vibe made its first steamy appearance way back 2011 on <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13335037.Divergent__Divergent___1_" title="Divergent (Divergent, #1) by Veronica Roth" rel="nofollow noopener">Divergent</a>. The first novella written in Four's perspective was <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13615258.Free_Four_Tobias_Tells_the_Story__Divergent___1_5_" title="Free Four Tobias Tells the Story (Divergent, #1.5) by Veronica Roth" rel="nofollow noopener">Free Four: Tobias Tells the Story</a> in which he described his feelings when he first met Abnegation-transfer <b> Tris Prior. </b> In this new novella comprised of like 50 pages, Tobias Eaton told his story as an Abnegation-born and the rules he had to live by with his father. He is a good narrator and I can personally feel his pain and fears while telling his story. I can't help but hate Marcus for inflicting him pain and even thought he could condition Tobias's mind to stay on his faction. Readers will also have a look on his Dauntless initiation and how he came to be called 'Four'. (but we all know that, really.)<br><br>I can't wait for the next novella. More Four!<br><br></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer18042868327890054854"><blockquote>
  <i>“You’re the one who has to live with your choice,” she says. “Everyone else will get over it, move on, no matter what you decide. But you never will.”</i>
</blockquote><br/>I'm apparently in a mood for short stories this week.This is Four's story and it's quite interesting.This is Four that we meet and fell in love with in Divergent-wreck,but a badass wreck.But we don't really learn anything new...Marcus is a seriously messed up person,I would actually like to know more about him and his relationship with Four,did</span>
  <span id="freeText18042868327890054854" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>“You’re the one who has to live with your choice,” she says. “Everyone else will get over it, move on, no matter what you decide. But you never will.”</i>
</blockquote><br>I'm apparently in a mood for short stories this week.This is Four's story and it's quite interesting.This is Four that we meet and fell in love with in Divergent-wreck,but a badass wreck.But we don't really learn anything new...Marcus is a seriously messed up person,I would actually like to know more about him and his relationship with Four,did he know that Four is Divergent?Did Four know that there's something wrong? So many questions,so little good informative material from Veronica Roth.<br>Overall,this was a cool short story.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1428588259ra/14448172.gif" width="250" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_2293626713" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2293626713" />
    <a title="Elizabeth" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1762033-elizabeth"><img alt="Elizabeth" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1491327487p2/1762033.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2293626713?book_show_action=true">Feb 12, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Elizabeth" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Elizabeth" href="/user/show/1762033-elizabeth">Elizabeth</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1762033-elizabeth?shelf=novella">novella</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1762033-elizabeth?shelf=dystopian">dystopian</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1762033-elizabeth?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1762033-elizabeth?shelf=series">series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2293626713" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11220789449635610715">I've only read the first installment of the <i>Divergent</i> series. Despite the fact that I didn't move forward with the other books, I actually find this world fascinating. Unfortunately the style of writing just isn't as strong as in, say, <i>The Hunger Games.</i><br/><br/>This is a decent look into Four's Dauntless initiation and will probably satisfy anyone who is invested in the series.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

It also includes his initiation and how he came to get his legendary nickname!</span>

<div id="review_644479222" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/644479222" />
    <a title="Mary" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10394863-mary"><img alt="Mary" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1373463422p2/10394863.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/644479222?book_show_action=true">Jun 18, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mary" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mary" href="/user/show/10394863-mary">Mary</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer644479222" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16674685981147840762"><b>
  <i>"My name is Four. Call me 'Stiff' again and you and I will have a problem."</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380425826ra/850138.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I can't even express how much I miss this world and especially one of my top book boyfriends, Four. It surely was a treat to get inside his head once again after I got a taste of it in <b>Free Four</b>. This story basically narrates how he came about to choosing to transfer to Dauntless to escape his life with his father in Abnegation. <br/><br/>What I loved most about this super mini novella is how it made Tobias/Four look more human</span>
  <span id="freeText16674685981147840762" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>"My name is Four. Call me 'Stiff' again and you and I will have a problem."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380425826ra/850138.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I can't even express how much I miss this world and especially one of my top book boyfriends, Four. It surely was a treat to get inside his head once again after I got a taste of it in <b>Free Four</b>. This story basically narrates how he came about to choosing to transfer to Dauntless to escape his life with his father in Abnegation. <br><br>What I loved most about this super mini novella is how it made Tobias/Four look more human <i>(and less of a god in my eyes lol)</i>. He didn't really start out to be this strong alpha-male that we know and love and instead, he was even this weak and fearful scrawny kid who just made the decision of choosing the lesser of two evils. In fact, he even appeared to be a tad bit weaker than Tris in some ways when he transferred to Dauntless, which just blew my mind away because of how far he'd come to be this strong and dependent leader that we know in Divergent and Insurgent. <br><br>I'm just itching to get my hands on the rest of the other Four novellas and more importantly... I needed <b>ALLEGIANT</b> like yesterday. </span>
  <a data-text-id="16674685981147840762" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('qzMWxFvp5kPSbTYWTZo3bxdvBqapQQ3uxpOZrdHHXLxjqXJ5ipomXQ0av0toUzXJVZ6VGPe9AKeUm+OaRJVu+g==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('6rKBoGH2zhgAxkDkb10isC661/JUZQQbtPGREg1TTmciKOUdsIUOBt+xyblKlCAWbEtETAqZCVLm+eslmAF8IQ==')})
  }
